*Taiki Miyagawa,Akinori F. Ebihara*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出基于生存分析的KM-ARL和KM-ADD非参数估计器，解决有限和不规则序列长度下QCD中ARL与ADD估计难题，具有渐近无偏性和实用价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ARL和ADD虽是QCD中重要的最优性准则，但在实际数据集中因序列长度有限且不规则而难以应用，亟需提出能处理此类情形的稳健估计方法。

Method: 将QCD中的检测问题类比为生存分析，利用Kaplan-Meier估计器建模检测概率，从而在序列截断条件下提出KM-ARL和KM-ADD非参数估计器，并推导其估计偏差界。

Result: 推导了估计偏差界，证明了除需外推情况外该估计器是渐近无偏的；模拟和真实数据实验验证了其在实际场景中的有效性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 所提方法显著提升了QCD在有限不规则序列下的可解释性与模型选择能力，并提供了开源Python工具包便于实践应用。

Abstract: We propose non-parametric estimators for the average run length (ARL) and average detection delay (ADD) in quickest changepoint detection (QCD) under finite and irregular sequence lengths. Although ARL and ADD are widely used as optimality criteria in theoretical and simulation studies, their application to real-world datasets is hindered by limited and irregular sequence lengths. To address this issue, we propose non-parametric estimators for the ARL and ADD, termed KM-ARL and KM-ADD, by drawing an analogy between QCD and survival analysis to model detection probabilities under sequence truncation. We derive estimation bias bounds and prove that they are asymptotically unbiased unless extrapolation is required. Experiments on simulated and real-world datasets demonstrate their practical utility, enhancing robustness against limited and irregular sequence lengths, improving interpretability, and facilitating empirical, intuitive model selection. Our Python code is provided at https://github.com/TaikiMiyagawa/Kaplan-Meier-Average-Run-Length, offering ready-to-use implementations for practitioners.

</details>


### [126] [Descriptive versus Regulatory Uncertainty in Bounded Predictive Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18909)
*Ahmed Gamal Eldin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文证明了当前Transformer架构在推理时只能产生“描述性不确定性”（无法递归影响策略），而非“调节性不确定性”（能直接进入优化景观驱动重构）。基于Landauer原理，在热力学层面解释了这一结构性缺陷：正确与错误的推理消耗相同能量。实验表明，3B/8B/70B参数模型的token级香农熵在不同任务间统计不变，而准确率从0%到100%变化；熵与准确率正交，且这一解耦具有尺度不变性。论文指出，真正的认知落地需要热力学底物状态与信息处理成本的物理耦合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究未阐明不确定性是否参与系统未来行为的动力学，抑或仅仅是描述输出分布而不产生后果。论文试图区分描述性不确定性与调节性不确定性，并检验当前Transformer是否具备后者。

Method: 理论证明结合实验验证。理论上基于Landauer原理论证调节性不确定性需要能量成本；实验上在3B/8B/70B三个本地部署的语言模型上测量token级香农熵，覆盖模式检索、因果算子应用和分布外因果泛化三类任务。

Result: 所有模型的token级香农熵在不同任务间统计不变（所有配对p >= 0.568，模型内范围0.011-0.028 nats），而任务准确率从0%到100%变化。熵与准确率正交，且解耦程度具有尺度不变性。

Conclusion: Transformer架构存在结构性缺陷，其不确定性是描述性的而非调节性的，无法通过增加参数或训练数据解决。真正的认知落地要求热力学底物状态与信息处理成本之间存在物理耦合。

Abstract: Any system that models the world under finite representational capacity must compress; any compression entails a prior; and the prior is the system's bias. What has not been established is whether uncertainty participates in the dynamics governing future behavior, or merely describes the output distribution without consequence. We introduce a structural distinction between descriptive uncertainty, which does not recursively modulate the system's policy, and regulatory uncertainty, which directly enters the optimization landscape and drives persistent adaptive restructuring. We prove formally that current transformer architectures are confined to descriptive uncertainty at inference. We ground this in thermodynamics via Landauer's principle: for uncertainty to be regulatory, epistemic error must cost real energy; in a decoupled system, hallucinations and correct derivations dissipate identical energy. We test this empirically across three locally-deployed language models (3B, 8B, 70B parameters). Token-level Shannon entropy is statistically invariant across tasks spanning pattern retrieval, causal operator application, and out-of-distribution causal generalization in all three models (all pairwise p >= 0.568; within-model ranges 0.011-0.028 nats), while task accuracy varies substantially across the same conditions (0%-100%). Entropy and accuracy are orthogonal. The decoupling is scale-invariant: larger models achieve higher accuracy but identical entropy flatness. This structural incapacity is not resolvable by additional parameters or training data. Genuine epistemic grounding requires physical coupling between thermodynamic substrate state and information processing cost.

</details>


### [127] [Simply Stabilizing the Loop via Fully Looped Transformer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18797)
*Rao Fu,Zixuan Yang,Jiankun Zhang,Jing Ma,Hechang Chen,Yu Li,Yi Chang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Fully Looped Transformer，通过全循环架构和注意力注入两种无参数修改，解决了Looped Transformer在增加循环次数时出现的梯度振荡和残差爆炸问题，实现了最多12次循环的稳定训练，并在下游任务上提升达13.2%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Looped Transformer通过循环复用相同Transformer块，在不增加参数量和上下文长度的情况下提升性能，但随循环次数增加会出现训练不稳定问题。作者分析发现不稳定性源于梯度振荡和残差爆炸，因此希望解决这两个问题以实现稳定训练。

Method: 提出两种无参数修改：(1) Fully Looped Architecture——将跨循环信号分布到所有层，缓解残差爆炸；(2) Attention Injection——复用现有注意力模块抑制梯度振荡。

Result: Fully Looped Transformer可稳定训练至12次循环，而基线模型在此设置下崩溃；在更温和的设置下，下游任务性能提升最高达13.2%。

Conclusion: Fully Looped Transformer提升了训练稳定性、下游性能，并可通过推理时调整循环次数来适应不同计算预算，展示了良好的可扩展性和实用性。

Abstract: Scaling model performance typically requires increasing model size. Looped Transformer offers a compelling alternative by iteratively reusing the same Transformer blocks, trading additional computation for improved performance without increasing parameter count or context length. Because the number of loop iterations can be adjusted at inference, it also provides a natural mechanism for balancing performance and test-time compute. However, Looped Transformer still suffers from training instability when the number of loop iterations increases. Our analysis reveals that this instability stems from two sources: gradient oscillation and residual explosion. To address these two problems, we propose the Fully Looped Transformer, which introduces two parameter-free modifications: (1) Fully Looped Architecture, which distributes inter-loop signals across all layers to mitigate residual explosion; (2) Attention Injection, which reuses the existing attention block to suppress gradient oscillation. These modifications stabilize training dynamics, enabling the Fully Looped Transformer to be trained stably up to 12 loop iterations, whereas other baseline looped models collapse in this regime. In milder settings where Looped Transformer does not collapse, Fully Looped Transformer still improves average downstream-task performance by up to 13.2\%. Overall, our experiments demonstrate that Fully Looped Transformer improves training stability, enhances downstream performance, and provides preliminary adaptability under different test-time compute budgets by varying loop iterations at inference.

</details>


### [128] [When Individually Calibrated Models Become Collectively Miscalibrated](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18858)
*Zhaohui Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文发现，在多智能体环境中，即使每个预测模型单独校准，当它们以Brier分数最优的博弈方式交互时，聚合预测会系统性失准（低估正类概率），产生"集体误校准"现象。VCG机制通过激励对齐解决了这一问题，在三个真实数据集上证明了鲁棒性和近最优性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战了一个常见但未被充分验证的假设：个体校准的模型聚合后仍然校准。作者发现这一假设在多智能体博弈场景（Brier最优局部响应）下不成立，即使没有故意协调，个体最优报告也会导致集体误校准。

Method: 理论分析了Brier分数聚合下，正相关信念导致个体低估正类概率的机制，证明了PoA > 1（当协方差>0时）。提出了VCG（Vickrey-Clarke-Groves）机制作为替代方案，通过奖励边际贡献实现激励相容。在NSL-KDD、UNSW-NB15和信用卡欺诈三个数据集上进行了实验验证。

Result: 在标准设定下（5个智能体，相关系数0.5，基率0.3），假阴性率的PoA达到7.25倍。VCG机制在真实数据集上保持了相当的准确率，同时提供了强鲁棒性，尤其在数据稀疏和对抗环境下表现优异，自适应加权进一步提升了分布漂移下的性能。

Conclusion: 个体校准不能保证聚合校准（在博弈交互下），VCG机制是解决这一集体误校准问题的有效方法，具备激励相容性和近最优性能。

Abstract: Probabilistic prediction systems often aggregate probability estimates from multiple models into a single decision. A common assumption is that if each model is individually calibrated, the aggregate prediction will also be well calibrated. We show that this assumption fails in multi-agent settings: individually calibrated predictors can become collectively miscalibrated when their predictions interact strategically, in the game-theoretic sense of Brier-optimal local response, even without deliberate coordination.
  This phenomenon arises naturally when agents are independently trained on overlapping data. We prove that under Brier-score-based aggregation with positively correlated beliefs, each agent's individually optimal report systematically underestimates the positive-class probability, yielding a Price of Anarchy greater than one whenever Cov(b_i, b_j) > 0.
  In a canonical setting (n = 5 agents, pairwise correlation = 0.5, base rate = 0.3), the empirically measured PoA in false-negative rate reaches 7.25x. In contrast, VCG-based aggregation aligns incentives by rewarding marginal contribution, achieving dominant-strategy incentive compatibility and near-optimal performance.
  Experiments on three real-world datasets (NSL-KDD, UNSW-NB15, Credit Card Fraud) show that VCG provides strong robustness while maintaining comparable accuracy. It performs particularly well in data-sparse and adversarial settings, and adaptive weighting further improves performance under distribution shift.

</details>


### [129] [WinQ: Accelerating Quantization-Aware Training of Language Models Around Saddle Points](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17471)
*Dongyue Li,Zechun Liu,Kai Yi,Zhenshuo Zhang,Changsheng Zhao,Raghuraman Krishnamoorthi,Harshit Khaitan,Hongyang R. Zhang,Steven Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文分析了量化感知训练(QAT)收敛缓慢的原因——权重收敛到鞍点周围的平坦区域，Hessian矩阵特征值集中在零附近且幅度小。提出WinQ算法：周期性重置权重到全精度与量化权重的线性插值，以及对注入噪声的权重计算梯度来正则化Hessian，加速QAT最高4倍，在子4比特量化上提升最高8.8%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: QAT在低位宽（低于4比特）下收敛缓慢且早期性能停滞，先前研究观察到该问题但未能明确其根本原因。本文旨在通过分析损失曲面Hessian矩阵的谱来揭示该现象的根源。

Method: (1) 通过估计损失曲面Hessian谱分析QAT收敛性；(2) 提出WinQ算法：①周期性将权重重置到全精度与量化权重的线性插值，减小到量化网格的距离并增大Hessian特征值幅度；②对注入噪声的权重计算梯度以正则化Hessian。

Result: WinQ将QAT加速最高4倍；相同训练成本下，在子4比特量化上提升SOTA最高8.8%；在16种不同设置（语言模型、量化方法、位宽）下结果一致。

Conclusion: QAT收敛缓慢的原因是权重收敛到鞍点周围的平坦区域（Hessian特征值正负均有且幅度小）。WinQ通过重置权重和噪声梯度正则化有效缓解了该问题，显著加速收敛并提升量化性能。

Abstract: Quantization-aware training (QAT) is widely adopted to quantize language models by training full-precision weights using gradients from the quantized model. The main bottleneck is its slow convergence and early performance plateau, particularly below 4-bit-widths. While this problem has been observed in prior work, its precise cause remains unclear. In this paper, we analyze the convergence of QAT by estimating the spectrum of the loss-surface Hessians. We find that the weights converge to flat regions around saddle points, where a large fraction of the Hessian eigenvalues are both positive and negative. During training, an increasing fraction of Hessian eigenvalues concentrates around zero, whose magnitude decreases. At lower bit-widths, the magnitude of eigenvalues in the Hessian spectrum is significantly smaller. To mitigate these issues, we propose an algorithm called WinQ to accelerate QAT, which involves: (1) periodically resetting weights to the linear interpolation of full-precision and quantized weights, reducing the distance to the quantization grid and increasing eigenvalue magnitude, and (2) computing gradients of noise-injected weights to regularize the Hessian. Extensive experiments show that WinQ accelerates QAT by up to 4 times across various quantization methods and models. Under the same training cost, WinQ improves state-of-the-art sub-4-bit quantization by up to 8.8%. These results are consistent across 16 settings with different language models, quantization methods, and bit widths.

</details>


### [130] [ReCrit: Transition-Aware Reinforcement Learning for Scientific Critic Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18799)
*Wanghan Xu,Yuhao Zhou,Hengyuan Zhao,Shuo Li,Dianzhi Yu,Zhenfei Yin,Yaowen Hu,Fengli Xu,Wanli Ouyang,Wenlong Zhang,Lei Bai*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出ReCrit框架，将大模型批评交互建模为初始到批评状态间的正确性转换问题，通过四象限划分（修正、谄媚、鲁棒性、边界）和强化学习训练，显著提升科学推理中模型对用户批评的正确响应能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大模型在与用户的批评交互中不仅会答错，还会在受到批评后放弃正确的科学解答，这在科学推理场景中尤其危险。传统方法只关注最终答案的准确率，忽视了交互过程中正确性转换的关键问题。

Method: 提出ReCrit框架，将初始答案到批评后回答的行为分解为四个象限：修正（Correction）、谄媚（Sycophancy）、鲁棒性（Robustness）和边界（Boundary）。对修正和鲁棒性给予奖励，对谄媚进行惩罚，将持续错误作为弱边界信号。同时采用动态异步 rollout 和尾自适应补全机制减少交互训练中的等待开销。

Result: 在ChemBench、TRQA、EarthSE三个科学推理基准上，Qwen3.5-4B模型批评准确率从38.15提升至51.49，Qwen3.5-9B模型从45.40提升至55.59。消融实验表明，传统最终答案奖励提供极少交互增益，而转换感知奖励和象限加权能产生更可区分的训练信号。

Conclusion: ReCrit通过转换感知强化学习有效提升了大模型在科学推理中的批评交互能力，揭示了正确性转换建模比最终答案准确率更适合评估交互质量。

Abstract: Large language models can fail in critic interaction not only by answering incorrectly, but also by abandoning an initially correct scientific solution after user criticism. This is especially risky in scientific reasoning, where user criticism can turn a valid answer into an incorrect one. We frame critic interaction as an inter-turn correctness-transition problem rather than a final-answer accuracy problem, and identify three challenges: transition awareness, decoupling useful correction from harmful sycophancy, and scalable rollout. We propose ReCrit, a transition-aware reinforcement learning framework that decomposes Initial-to-Critic behavior into four quadrants: Correction, Sycophancy, Robustness, and Boundary. ReCrit rewards correction and robustness, penalizes sycophancy, and treats persistent errors as weak boundary signals. To make interaction training practical, ReCrit further uses dynamic asynchronous rollout with tail-adaptive completion to reduce rollout waiting. On three scientific reasoning benchmarks, ChemBench, TRQA, and EarthSE, ReCrit improves average Critic accuracy from 38.15 to 51.49 on Qwen3.5-4B and from 45.40 to 55.59 on Qwen3.5-9B. Ablations show that final-answer rewards provide little interaction-level gain, while transition-aware rewards and quadrant weighting produce more distinguishable training signals and larger net Critic-stage improvement. The code is available at https://github.com/black-yt/ReCrit .

</details>

Motivation: 现有可控制帕累托前沿学习(CPFL)方法缺乏对约束条件下超网络训练的严格理论保证，分割可行性条件(split feasibility conditions)下的约束多目标优化问题尚未被解决。

Method: 1) 将约束帕累托问题重构为双层次标量分裂问题(BSSP)；2) 提出自适应平衡惩罚(ABP)算法，包含最优性、集合可行性和图像可行性三个梯度分量，通过可计算下界驱动的自适应指示器动态平衡；3) 利用凸替代技术证明标准凸性和Robbins-Monro步长假设下的全序列收敛；4) 将ABP惩罚结构转化为两阶段"可行性优先"训练策略，应用于Hyper-MLP和HyperTrans架构。

Result: 在5个多目标基准上验证了ABP求解器的有效性；在3个多任务学习数据集上，ABP-HyperNet将约束可行性从36-49%提升至87-100%，EFHV指标相比无约束基线提升高达2.3倍。

Conclusion: ABP算法及其超网络实现为约束CPFL提供了理论保证与实用框架，显著提升了约束可行性，为实际多目标优化中处理约束提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: We address the open problem of training hypernetworks for Controllable Pareto Front Learning (CPFL) under split feasibility conditions with rigorous theoretical guarantees. We reformulate the constrained Pareto problem as a Bi-Level Scalarized Split Problem (BSSP) and propose the Adaptive Balanced Penalty (ABP) algorithm, whose three gradient components -- optimality, set feasibility, and image feasibility -- are blended through an adaptive indicator driven by a computable lower bound. Using a novel convex surrogate technique, we prove full-sequence convergence under standard convexity and Robbins-Monro step-size assumptions. The ABP penalty structure is then translated into a two-phase, feasibility-first training strategy for Hyper-MLP and HyperTrans architectures (ABP-HyperNet). To evaluate constrained CPFL, we introduce the Expected Feasible Hypervolume (EFHV), which jointly captures solution quality and constraint satisfaction. Experiments on five multi-objective benchmarks validate the ABP solver against ground truth, while three multi-task learning datasets demonstrate that ABP-HyperNet achieves up to 2.3x higher EFHV than unconstrained baselines by raising feasibility from 36-49% to 87-100%.

</details>


### [134] [Theory-optimal Quantization Based on Flatness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18800)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有后训练量化方法在处理激活异常值时效果有限，即使经过线性变换，权值和激活值仍存在集中的异常值分布模式，严重损害低比特精度下的模型性能。

Method: 首先建立量化误差与异常值之间的数学关系模型，提出新的指标Flatness来量化异常值分布情况；基于该指标推导出理论最优解；提出BDQ框架，通过学习优化的对角变换操作，将异常值分布分散到矩阵的各维度上。

Conclusion: BDQ建立了新的量化基准，有效解决了低比特量化中的异常值分布问题，在多种困难设定下均取得了显著提升。

Abstract: Post-training quantization has emerged as a widely adopted technique for compressing and accelerating the inference of Large Language Models (LLMs). The primary challenges in LLMs quantization stem from activation outliers, which significantly degrade model performance especially at lower bit precision. While recent approaches attempt to mitigate outliers through linear transformations across feature dimensions, our analysis reveals that the transformed weights and activations still exhibit persistent outlier patterns with concentrated magnitude distributions. In this paper, we first model the mathematical relationship between quantization error and outliers, and then introduce a new metric Flatness to quantify the distribution of outliers. Based on this, we derive the theoretical optimal solution with respect to Flatness. Building on these insights, we propose Bidirectional Diagonal Quantization (BDQ), a novel post-training quantization framework that effectively disperses outlier patterns through optimized matrix transformations. BDQ strategically distributes outlier magnitudes across matrix dimensions via learned diagonal operations. Extensive experiments demonstrate that BDQ establishes a new quantization benchmark. It achieves less than 1\% accuracy drop in W4A4 quantization on the LLaMA-3-8B model. In the more challenging W2A4KV16 experiment, compared to state-of-the-art approaches, BDQ reduces the performance gap by 39.1\% on the DeepSeek-R1-Distill-LLaMA-70B model.

### [135] [DeRegiME: Deep Regime Mixtures for Probabilistic Forecasting under Distribution Shift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19231)
*Kieran Wood,Stefan Zohren,Stephen J. Roberts*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出DeRegiME，一种基于稀疏高斯过程的多层概率预测模型，通过非平稳核混合和Student-t似然，将残差不确定性分解为可解释的隐状态机制，在10个基准数据集上NLPD提升20.3%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经预测模型（如DeepAR）主要关注点预测，概率头部（单一边际分布、混合分布、分位数集或扩散样本）很少暴露残差的隐状态结构，而在含噪异方差时间序列中，分布偏移往往出现在残差不确定性而非条件均值中。

Method: 提出Deep Regime Mixture of Experts (DeRegiME)，核心是使用一个稀疏变分高斯过程（sparse GP），其非平稳机制混合核（regime-mixing kernel）通过共享门控（shared gate）组合每个机制的子核和噪声（Student-t似然），得到单个稀疏GP后验（而非混合GP专家）。有效机制数由stick-breaking门控自动剪枝。特征空间采用直和分解，机制作为残差相似性聚类，其转换表现为隐式变点。

Result: 在10个基准数据集和3种编码器网格上，DeRegiME相比最强的编码器匹配基线（DeepAR/GluonTS风格的动态Student-t头部）NLPD提升20.3%，CRPS提升3.0%，MSE提升4.7%。改进在包含突变、渐变和季节性偏移的所有数据集上一致。

Conclusion: DeRegiME通过可解释的均值-残差-噪声分解，有效捕获了多步预测中的隐状态不确定性结构，在概率预测质量上显著优于现有方法，且具有理论保证（核有效性和预测密度合规性）。

Abstract: We introduce DeRegiME -- Deep Regime Mixture of Experts -- a direct multi-horizon probabilistic forecaster that separates latent uncertainty regimes from the underlying signal and softly assigns each forecast location to learned recurring regimes using a sparse variational Gaussian process (GP) whose nonstationary regime-mixing kernel and Student-t likelihood combine per-regime sub-kernels and noise processes via a shared gate. This yields a single sparse-GP posterior, not a mixture of GP experts. DeRegiME addresses a key limitation of neural forecasters: point forecasts discard residual uncertainty, and probabilistic heads -- whether single marginals, uninterpreted mixtures, quantile sets, or diffusion samples -- rarely expose the regime structure of the residual. Yet distribution shift in noisy heteroskedastic time series may be abrupt, gradual, or horizon-dependent and often appears in residual uncertainty rather than the conditional mean. DeRegiME yields an interpretable mean-residual-noise decomposition with a direct-sum feature-space representation that anchors regimes as clusters of residual similarity whose transitions surface as implicit changepoints. The effective number of regimes is pruned by the stick-breaking gate. We prove kernel validity and predictive-density propriety, and across ten benchmarks and three encoder grids DeRegiME improves negative log predictive density (NLPD) by 20.3% over the strongest encoder-matched baseline, a DeepAR/GluonTS-style dynamic Student-t head, with parallel gains on CRPS (3.0%) and MSE (4.7%). Improvements are consistent across all datasets, which span abrupt, gradual, and seasonal shifts.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Muon优化器虽在矩阵参数模型（如大语言模型）中收敛更快，但其泛化性质尚未被理论研究，本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 基于算法稳定性和数学归纳法分析Muon的泛化误差；提出MiMuon优化器，通过谨慎使用梯度正交化将Muon与带动量的SGD混合，并同时分析其收敛性质。

Result: Muon泛化误差为$O(1/(Nκ^T))$，MiMuon泛化误差降至$O(1/N)$，且两者收敛率均为$O(1/T^{1/4})$；在Qwen3-0.6B和YOLO26m上验证了有效性。

Abstract: Matrix-structured parameters frequently appear in many artificial intelligence models such as large language models. More recently, an efficient Muon optimizer is designed for matrix parameters of large-scale models, and shows markedly faster convergence than the vector-wise algorithms. Although some works have begun to study convergence properties (i.e., optimization error) of the Muon optimizer, its generalization properties (i.e., generalization error) is still not established. Thus, in this paper, we study generalization error of the Muon optimizer based on algorithmic stability and mathematical induction, and prove that the Muon has a generalization error of $O\big(\frac{1}{Nκ^{T}}\big)$, where $N$ is training sample size, and $T$ denotes iteration number, and $κ>0$ denotes minimum difference between singular values of gradient estimate. To enhance generalization of the Muon, we propose an effective mixed Muon (MiMuon) optimizer by cautiously using orthogonalization of gradient, which is a hybrid of Muon and momentum-based SGD optimizers. Then we prove that our MiMuon optimizer has a lower generalization error of $O\big(\frac{1}{N}\big)$ than $O\big(\frac{1}{Nκ^{T}}\big)$ of Muon optimizer, since $κ$ generally is very small. Meanwhile, we also studied the convergence properties of our MiMuon algorithm, and prove that our MiMuon algorithm has the same convergence rate of $O(\frac{1}{T^{1/4}})$ as the Muon algorithm. Some numerical experimental results on training large models including Qwen3-0.6B and YOLO26m demonstrate efficiency of the MiMuon optimizer.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 被动演示数据系统性欠采样罕见但关键的交互转换，导致动作条件世界模型在这些高影响力场景中不可靠，而提升鲁棒性需要主动诱发模型失败而非等待自然发生。

Method: 1) KL约束对抗课程：训练策略主动暴露世界模型高误差轨迹，同时保持接近行为分布；2) 对抗训练循环：持续微调世界模型于对抗发现的轨迹；3) PRIORITIZED ADVERSARIAL TRAJECTORY (PAT)缓冲区：基于预测误差、动作保真度和学习进度重新排序轨迹，聚焦未解决的失败模式。

Abstract: Modern action-conditioned video world models achieve strong short-horizon visual realism, yet remain unreliable on rare, interaction-critical transitions that dominate downstream planning and policy performance. Because passive demonstration data systematically under-samples these high-impact regimes, improving robustness requires actively eliciting model failures rather than relying on their natural occurrence. We introduce a KL-constrained adversarial curriculum in which a policy is trained to expose high-error trajectories of a diffusion-based world model while remaining close to the behavior distribution. The world model is continuously fine-tuned on these adversarially discovered trajectories, yielding an adversarial training loop that converts rare failures into a stable, near-distribution training signal without drifting into out-of-distribution exploitation. To maintain pressure on unresolved weaknesses as the model improves, we propose a Prioritized Adversarial Trajectory (PAT) buffer that re-ranks trajectories based on prediction error, action fidelity, and learning progress, focusing training on unresolved failure modes rather than repeatedly revisiting solved cases. We implement our approach in the MineRL framework and evaluate it on held-out out-of-distribution trajectories; PROWL improves robustness over models trained on passive data alone, reveals reward-hacking behaviors under weak behavioral constraints, and demonstrates that effective adversarial world-model training critically depends on balancing exploratory failure discovery with explicit behavioral regularization. Our results suggest that scalable world models benefit not only from larger datasets, but also from selectively generating informative training data.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有在线学习做市问题假设完全删失反馈，但真实限价订单簿中未成交时仍能揭示供需信息。作者希望量化这种额外信息对学习问题可学习性的根本性影响。

Method: 1) 随机i.i.d.市场：提出基于消去的算法，无需估值分布平滑假设即可达到O(√T)遗憾。2) 均值回复过程：考虑局部自回归和全局漂移条件，利用新的集中不等式证明O(√T)遗憾。3) 对抗性市场：设计探索-扰动算法，实现O(T^{2/3})期望遗憾。

Result: 在随机设定下达到高概率O(√T)遗憾，在均值回复设定下也达到O(√T)遗憾，在对抗性设定下达到O(T^{2/3})遗憾。证明了行动依赖反馈相比标准赌博机反馈能显著改进遗憾界。

Abstract: We study an online market-making problem in which a learner sequentially posts bid and ask prices for a single asset while interacting with traders holding private valuations. Unlike existing online learning formulations that assume fully censored feedback, we introduce an action-dependent feedback model inspired by real limit order books: when a trade occurs, the trader's valuation remains hidden, whereas when no trade occurs, informative feedback about supply and demand is revealed.
  We show that this additional information fundamentally changes the learnability of the problem. In the stochastic setting with i.i.d. market prices, we propose an elimination-based algorithm that achieves $O(\sqrt T)$ regret with high probability, without requiring any smoothness assumptions on the distribution of trader valuations. We then extend this result to a broad class of mean-reverting price processes by considering both local, autoregressive dynamics and a weaker global drift condition based on cumulative deviations from the mean. Under either assumption, we establish high-probability $O(\sqrt T)$ regret bounds, relying on a new concentration inequality of independent interest. Finally, in the adversarial setting with oblivious prices, we design an explore-then-perturb algorithm that guarantees $O(T^{2/3})$ regret in expectation.
  Our results quantify the value of observing the order book in online market making and demonstrate that even limited, action-dependent feedback can substantially improve regret guarantees compared to standard bandit feedback models.

Motivation: 探索大语言模型内部如何组合低层文学原语来生成具有情感和风格的文本，理解模型从词汇到情感的层次化组合机制。

Method: 使用稀疏自编码器（SAE）对两个模型的中层残差流进行特征提取，采用三阶段验证流水线（logit-lens探测、LLM评分、5-LLM评判面板），基于Cowen-Keltner 27类情感分类体系进行系统评估。

Result: Llama实现完整的27/27情感分类覆盖，Gemma达到23/27（仅"爱慕"缺失）；随机评判的通过概率约为10⁻³量级，非偶然；情感生成存在跨架构不对称性（Llama更直接命名情感，Gemma通过场景意象引发情感）。

Conclusion: 大语言模型内部存在可解释的文学原语组合架构，命名门控与自我特征分别承担不同的情感表达角色，且不同架构在情感表达策略上存在系统性差异。

Abstract: We characterize a compositional architecture of literary primitives in two instruction-tuned large language models (Llama 3.1 8B-Instruct and Gemma 2 9B-IT) via sparse autoencoders on mid-depth residual streams. Four feature classes emerge: naming-gates that promote lexical tokens of a target affect, an eleven-self cluster of first-person register features, stylistic register modulators (show-don't-tell and defamiliarization), and compositional emotions that arise only from multi-feature steering. Under a forced-choice 5-LLM judge panel applied to a 27-category emotion taxonomy (Cowen-Keltner), Llama reaches full 27/27 coverage by combining naming-gates, multi-feature recipes, and single self-feature steering; Gemma reaches 23/27 with adoration as the single residual strict-fail. Under random judging, the per-cell pass probability is on the order of $10^{-3}$ and the expected number of two-seed false-positive cells across the catalog is negligible, so the observed coverage is not consistent with chance. A cross-architectural asymmetry sits in the strict-versus-soft judge contrast: on the same generations, judges agree more often on Llama outputs than on Gemma outputs because Llama outputs name the target affect more directly while Gemma outputs evoke it through scene and imagery. Both architectures contain self-features that serve simultaneously as register markers and as emotion emitters, including a single most-RLHF-loaded self-feature per architecture that intensifies the institutional Helper-AI persona at one operating regime and produces affect-categorizable output at the same calibrated coefficient. Methodologically, the paper presents a three-stage validation pipeline (logit-lens, LLM-rate, 5-LLM judge) with documented anti-patterns; the total compute is single-GPU and about 15 minutes per emotion-feature discovery cycle.

### [143] [Metric-Gradient Projection for Stable Multi-Agent Policy Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18809)
*Zuyuan Zhang,Sizhe Tang,Mahdi Imani,Tian Lan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: HPML通过Hodge投影将多智能体系统的联合更新场分解为度量-梯度分量和循环交互分量，并沿度量-梯度分量更新，从而提升多智能体强化学习的稳定性和性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体学习中，各智能体的策略更新相互耦合，导致联合更新场中存在不可积的循环交互分量，使学习过程缓慢或不稳定。现有方法（正则化、信用分配、共识等）通过局部或算法层面的修改来稳定MARL，但缺乏对联合更新场几何结构的系统性处理。

Method: HPML将多智能体系统的联合更新场视为L^2向量场空间中的元素，通过Hodge型投影将其分解为度量-梯度势流（可积部分）和循环分量（不可积部分），仅沿投影后的度量-梯度分量更新。该投影通过变分定义、Poisson型方程刻画，并采用基于图的和摊销神经网络两种实现方式从样本中恢复投影方向。

Result: 理论方面，证明了投影动力学存在Lyapunov势函数，并给出了带有显式非势项加性界的均衡间隙界。实验方面，受控实验验证了几何机制的有效性，CTDE基准测试表明HPML作为插件式投影层能提升MARL管道的稳定性和归一化回报。

Conclusion: HPML提供了一种几何视角下的多智能体学习优化方法，通过分解联合更新场来消除循环交互的负面影响，可作为一种即插即用的模块与现有MARL算法结合，提升学习稳定性和性能。

Abstract: General-sum multi-agent learning is often governed by a stacked update field in which each agent's policy update changes the optimization landscape faced by the others. This coupling can entangle an integrable component of collective improvement with cyclic interaction dynamics, leading to slow or unstable multi-agent learning. Existing approaches, such as regularization, credit assignment, and consensus methods, stabilize MARL through local or algorithmic modifications; HPML complements them by projecting the joint update field onto a metric-gradient component. We introduce \textbf{HPML} (\textbf{H}odge-\textbf{P}rojected \textbf{M}ulti-agent \textbf{L}earning), which views the joint update field of a multi-agent system as an element of an $L^2$ space of vector fields and computes a Hodge-type projection onto the closest metric-gradient potential flow. HPML follows the projected component as the update direction, yielding the closest metric-gradient field under the chosen metric and sampling measure. The projection is defined variationally, characterized by a Poisson-type equation, and implemented through graph-based and amortized neural realizations that recover projected directions from samples. We show that the projected dynamics admit a Lyapunov potential and yield equilibrium-gap bounds with an explicit additive non-potentiality term. Controlled experiments validate the geometric mechanism, and CTDE benchmarks show improved stability and normalized return when HPML is used as a plug-in projection layer in MARL pipelines.

### [144] [D-PACE: Dynamic Position-Aware Cross-Entropy for Parallel Speculative Drafting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18810)
*Tianyu Wu,Yu Yao,Zhenting Qi,Han Zheng,Zhuohan Wang,Haoran Ma,Lawrence Liao,Himabindu Lakkaraju,Ju Li,Yilun Du*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有并行草稿模型在训练时使用固定的位置依赖加权策略（如头依赖权重或块位置衰减），无法随训练过程自适应调整，导致训练信号分配不合理。

Method: 从期望接受草稿长度的可微代理出发，推导出每个位置的训练权重，使其与该位置的对数概率梯度贡献相匹配，提出D-PACE（动态位置感知交叉熵）损失函数。

Result: 在6个基准测试、2种草稿模型深度、2种解码温度和2种目标模型上，D-PACE一致提升墙钟加速比和平均发射长度，训练时间开销仅2.3%，且不改变草稿架构和推理流程。

Conclusion: D-PACE通过动态位置感知加权有效提升了推测解码的性能，方法轻量且通用。

Abstract: Speculative decoding accelerates LLM inference by having a small drafter propose tokens that a larger target model verifies in parallel. Recent diffusion-based parallel drafters such as DFlash predict the full B-token block in one forward pass, enabling deeper drafters and longer accepted blocks. However, existing multi-token drafter objectives often use fixed position-dependent weighting schedules, such as head-dependent weights or block-position decays, which do not adapt as the positions limiting acceptance change during training. To address this, we derive per-position training weights from a differentiable surrogate of expected accepted draft length, matching the weight of each position to its log-probability gradient contribution. The resulting loss, D-PACE (Dynamic Position-Aware Cross-Entropy), shifts training signal toward positions that currently limit acceptance as the drafter improves. Across six benchmarks, two Qwen3-4B draft depths, two decoding temperatures, and two additional target models, D-PACE consistently improves both wall-clock speedup and average emitted length, with 2.3\% measured training-time overhead and no changes to the drafter architecture or inference procedure.

### [145] [PASC: Pipeline-Aware Conformal Prediction with Joint Coverage Guarantees for Multi-Stage NLP and LLM Pipelines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18812)
*Varun Kotte*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出PASC方法，将多阶段流水线的联合覆盖保证转化为单一标量共形预测问题，在NER→NED→实体类型流水线上达到96.4%端到端覆盖率，比Bonferroni方法（93.4%）和独立CP（86.5%）更优，且保持相同预测集大小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有NLP/LLM流水线（如NER→NED→实体类型、RAG、Agent链）中错误会跨阶段累积，但现有不确定性量化方法要么独立校准各阶段（无联合覆盖保证），要么使用Bonferroni联合界（保守且过紧），缺乏高效且非保守的联合覆盖方法。

Method: 提出PASC（Pipeline-Aware Split Conformal），将多阶段联合覆盖问题转化为单一标量共形预测问题，基于联合最大非一致性分数（joint maximum nonconformity score）进行校准，只需单次分位数计算。

Result: 在三阶段NER→NED→实体类型流水线上，PASC达到96.4%端到端覆盖率（Bonferroni 93.4%，独立CP 86.5%），相同平均预测集大小（1.083）；分布偏移下独立CP降至59%，PASC仍维持目标覆盖率；速度比Bonferroni快1.7倍；可扩展至K=6阶段（独立CP仅0.53%覆盖率）。

Conclusion: PASC提供了有限样本、分布无关的联合覆盖保证（所有K阶段同时被覆盖的概率≥1-α），紧致性达到1/(n+1)因子，可直接应用于复合LLM系统和Agent流水线。

Abstract: Modern NLP and LLM systems are pipelines: named entity recognition (NER) -> entity disambiguation (NED) -> entity typing, retrieval-augmented generation (retriever -> reader), and agentic chains of planner -> tool -> critic. Errors compound across stages, but existing uncertainty quantification methods either calibrate each stage independently (no joint coverage) or apply a Bonferroni union bound (joint coverage, but conservative). We present PASC (Pipeline-Aware Split Conformal), which reduces multi-stage joint coverage to a single scalar conformal prediction problem on the joint maximum nonconformity score. PASC provides a finite-sample distribution-free guarantee that all K stages are simultaneously covered with probability at least 1 - alpha, and is nearly tight up to a 1/(n+1) factor. On a three-stage NER -> NED -> entity-typing pipeline over CoNLL-2003, PASC achieves 96.4% end-to-end coverage versus 93.4% for Bonferroni and 86.5% for independent CP, at identical average prediction set size (1.083). Under distribution shift to WNUT-17 Twitter and WikiNEuRal Wikipedia data, PASC empirically maintains the target coverage in the tested shift settings while independent CP collapses to 59%. PASC requires a single quantile computation, runs 1.7x faster than Bonferroni, and scales to K = 6 stages where independent CP drops to 0.53 end-to-end coverage. The same joint-maximum-score reduction applies directly to compound LLM systems and agent pipelines.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有世界模型架构面临记忆权衡：Transformer保持局部细节但受限于二次注意力机制，循环和状态空间模型虽扩展性好但压缩历史导致保真度下降。本文旨在克服这一根本性权衡。

Method: 提出扩散框架，通过对比产品-of-experts（contrastive product-of-experts）整合三个互补专家：短期记忆专家（捕捉局部动态）、长期记忆专家（通过轻量测试时微调存储情景记忆）、空间长期记忆专家（强制几何与空间一致性）。

Conclusion: 建立了一种构建和运行记忆增强扩散世界模型的新范式，有效解耦了未来-过去一致性与单一架构之间的依赖关系。

Abstract: World models aim to predict plausible futures consistent with past observations, a capability central to planning and decision-making in reinforcement learning. Yet, existing architectures face a fundamental memory trade-off: transformers preserve local detail but are bottlenecked by quadratic attention, while recurrent and state-space models scale more efficiently but compress history at the cost of fidelity. To overcome this trade-off, we suggest decoupling future-past consistency from any single architecture and instead leveraging a set of specialized experts. We introduce a diffusion-based framework that integrates heterogeneous memory models through a contrastive product-of-experts formulation. Our approach instantiates three complementary roles: a short-term memory expert that captures fine local dynamics, a long-term memory expert that stores episodic history in external diffusion weights via lightweight test-time finetuning, and a spatial long-term memory expert that enforces geometric and spatial coherence. This compositional design avoids mode collapse and scales to long contexts without incurring a quadratic cost. Across simulated and real-world benchmarks, our method improves temporal consistency, recall of past observations, and navigation performance, establishing a novel paradigm for building and operating memory-augmented diffusion world models.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 不规则多变量时间序列在长时域预测中面临两难：离散方法通过重网格化会扭曲时间结构，而连续模型依赖顺序求解器易产生漂移。作者希望弥合这一差距。

Method: 提出Latent Laplace Diffusion (LLapDiff)框架：(1) 将目标建模为低维潜在轨迹，实现全时域生成；(2) 利用随机端口-哈密顿动力学指导逆过程，在拉普拉斯域通过可学习的复共轭极点参数化均值演化；(3) 通过更新-平均分析将采样间隙映射为有效事件域极点，设计间隙感知的历史总结器。

Abstract: Irregular multivariate time series impose a trade-off for long-horizon forecasting: discrete methods can distort temporal structure via re-gridding, while continuous-time models often require sequential solvers prone to drift. To bridge this gap, we present Latent Laplace Diffusion (LLapDiff), a generative framework that models the target as a low-dimensional latent trajectory, enabling horizon-wide generation without step-by-step integration over physical time. We guide the reverse process utilizing a stable modal parameterization motivated by stochastic port-Hamiltonian dynamics, and parameterize its mean evolution in the Laplace domain via learnable complex-conjugate poles, enabling direct evaluation over irregular timestamps. We also link continuous dynamics to irregular observations through renewal-averaging analysis, which maps sampling gaps to effective event-domain poles and motivates a gap-aware history summarizer. Extensive experiments show that LLapDiff improves over baselines in long-horizon forecasting, and its continuous-time generative nature supports missing-value imputation by querying the same model at historical timestamps. Code is available at https://github.com/pixelhero98/LLapDiffusion.

### [148] [How Faithful Is Trajectory-Based Data Attribution? Error Sources, Remedies, and Practical Guidelines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18814)
*Junwei Deng,Pingbang Hu,Suliang Jin,Hao Lu,Jiachen T. Wang,Shichang Zhang,Jiaqi W. Ma*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文首次系统分析了基于轨迹的数据归因方法中的三类误差来源（配置级、算法级、系统级），提出AdamW-influence方法解决了优化器不匹配问题，并通过K步前瞻框架为实际应用提供了可操作的指南。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轨迹数据归因方法广泛应用于数据选择、估值和模型诊断，但缺乏全面的误差分析，这引发了对方法忠实性的担忧，阻碍了可靠部署。

Method: 将总误差分为三类：配置级（优化器不匹配）、算法级（一阶泰勒近似）、系统级。提出AdamW-influence适配AdamW优化器，推导了算法误差的闭式代理，并构建了K步前瞻的统一框架。

Result: AdamW-influence在MLP、CNN、GPT-2、Llama 3.2-1B四种设置下，Spearman相关性提升10%到300%以上。算法误差与学习率和轨迹长度相关，在线选择策略在短视距下可与离线策略匹敌。

Conclusion: 通过系统误差分析和对策，将轨迹归因方法转化为实用的数据选择指南，建议联合调整视距和学习率以优化性能。

Abstract: Trajectory-based data attribution methods estimate the influence of training samples on model predictions by unrolling the training trajectory. They are widely used in applications such as data selection, data valuation, and model diagnosis, but there is a lack of comprehensive error analysis of these methods, raising concerns about method faithfulness and hindering reliable deployment. In this work, we provide the first systematic analysis of error sources in trajectory-based data attribution, together with concrete remedies to mitigate them and practical guidelines for downstream use. We organize the total error into three categories, config-level, algorithm-level, and system-level. We make three contributions. First, we identify optimizer mismatch as the dominant config-level error: existing methods derive their attribution under the assumption of SGD, even for models trained with the modern de facto optimizer AdamW. We propose AdamW-influence to fully account for AdamW's optimization dynamics, yielding improvements from 10% to over 300% in Spearman correlation between estimated and ground-truth influence across four settings spanning MLP, CNN, GPT-2, and Llama 3.2-1B. Second, we isolate the remaining algorithm-level error arising from the first-order Taylor approximation, identify the learning rate and trajectory length as factors governing the error magnitude, and derive a closed-form error proxy that can be evaluated along the original trajectory without retraining. Third, we translate these insights into practical guidelines for data selection by unifying offline and online strategies under a K-step look-ahead framework. Under this framework, online selection with a short horizon often matches or exceeds offline, and the optimal horizon can be tuned jointly with the learning rate. Together, these results turn the framework into an actionable selection recipe for practitioners.

### [149] [FLUXtrapolation: A benchmark on extrapolating ecosystem fluxes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19812)
*Anya Fries,Jacob A Nelson,Martin Jung,Markus Reichstein,Jonas Peters*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FLUXtrapolation是一个用于评估生态系统通量外推的基准测试，专为处理渐进式分布偏移而设计。它通过时间、空间和温度三种外推场景，结合多尺度评估（包括尾部误差），揭示了现有基线方法在中位数RMSE上表现相似但在尾部误差上存在显著差异，为机器学习方法在分布偏移下的评估提供了真实且有意义的挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生态系统通量（碳、水、能量循环）只能通过稀疏分布的测量塔直接观测，全球通量估计需要利用观测站点数据训练模型并在未观测区域进行预测（即升尺度）。这一过程面临严重的领域泛化问题：协变量分布在不同气候、生态系统类型和环境条件下存在偏移，同时条件分布也存在偏移（重要驱动变量在全球尺度上不可观测）。现有基准无法充分捕捉这些复杂的分布偏移，因此需要专门设计的基准来推动相关方法的发展。

Method: FLUXtrapolation基于通量升尺度的领域专业知识设计，定义了三种外推场景：时间外推、空间外推和基于温度的外推。评估方式涵盖：保留域上的性能、多时间尺度聚合评估以及尾部误差评估。作者对协变量分布偏移和条件分布偏移进行了定量分析，并通过试点研究对比了多种基线方法的表现。

Result: 在试点研究中发现：基线方法在小时级中位数RMSE上表现相似，难以区分；但在所提出的尾部误差和多尺度评估指标下，不同方法之间出现明显分化。

Conclusion: FLUXtrapolation为分布偏移下的机器学习方法提供了一个真实且具有实际意义的挑战基准。在该基准上取得进展将直接支持改进通量升尺度的科学目标，有助于更准确地理解全球碳、水和能量循环。

Abstract: We introduce FLUXtrapolation, a benchmark for extrapolating ecosystem fluxes under progressively harder distribution shifts. Ecosystem fluxes are central to understanding the carbon, water, and energy cycles, yet they can only be measured directly at sparsely located measurement towers. Producing global flux estimates therefore requires training models on observed sites using globally available covariates and predicting in unobserved regions, that is, upscaling. Flux upscaling is a challenging domain generalization problem that is affected by a shift in covariate distribution across climates, ecosystem types, and environmental conditions, as well as by conditional shift: important drivers remain unobserved at global scale. We provide a quantitative analysis of both these shifts in $P_X$ and $P_{Y\mid X}$. FLUXtrapolation is designed based on domain expertise on flux upscaling: it defines temporal, spatial, and temperature-based extrapolation scenarios and evaluates performance across held-out domains, temporal aggregations, and tail errors. In a pilot study, we find that baselines perform similarly under median hourly RMSE, but separate under the proposed tail-focused and multi-scale evaluation. FLUXtrapolation therefore poses a realistic and thus relevant challenge for machine learning methods under distribution shift; at the same time, progress on this benchmark would directly support the scientific goal of improving flux upscaling.

### [150] [DynaTrain: Fast Online Parallelism Switching for Elastic LLM Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18815)
*Yuanqing Wang,Yuchen Zhang,Hao Lin,Junhao Hu,Chunyang Zhu,Quanlu Zhang,Boxun Li,Guohao Dai,Zhi Yang,Daning Cheng,Yunquan Zhang,Yu Wang*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有训练框架基于静态执行模型构建，无法应对LLM训练中资源波动、RLHF阶段切换和集群弹性等动态变化，导致最优并行布局持续变化，亟需支持在线重配置的分布式训练系统。

Method: 提出虚拟参数空间（VPS）抽象，将分布式训练状态统一到逻辑坐标空间，将并行配置映射为确定性映射，将复杂转换简化为几何交集计算；在此基础上构建状态路由与传输层（实现秩本地传输、内存感知、无死锁调度）和弹性设备管理器（将新世界构建与训练重叠以掩盖拓扑变化成本）。

Result: 在70B密集模型和235B MoE模型上，重配置时间分别为2秒和4.36秒，性能比基于检查点和弹性系统的最先进方案高出三个数量级，同时保持正确性。

Conclusion: DynaTrain通过VPS抽象和在线重配置机制，有效解决了LLM训练中动态环境下的并行布局优化问题，实现了高效、正确的分布式训练动态重配置。

Abstract: Modern large language model (LLM) training is inherently dynamic: resource fluctuations, RLHF phase shifts, and cluster elasticity continually reshape the optimal parallelism layout, posing a significant challenge to existing training frameworks built around a static execution model. We present DynaTrain, a distributed training system for sub-second, online reconfiguration across arbitrary multi-dimensional parallelism. At its core, we propose a Virtual Parameter Space (VPS) abstraction that unifies all distributed training states under one logical coordinate space, turning any parallelism configuration into a deterministic mapping and collapsing complex transition into manageable geometric intersections. On top of VPS, a state routing-and-transition layer executes rank-local transfers under a memory-aware, deadlock-free schedule, and an Elastic Device Manager overlaps new-world construction with ongoing training to mask topology-change cost. On dense and MoE models up to 235B parameters, DynaTrain reconfigures a 70B dense model in under 2s and a 235B MoE model in 4.36s, outperforming state-of-the-art checkpoint-based and elastic systems by up to three orders of magnitude while preserving correctness.

### [151] [Smooth Piecewise Cutting for Neural Operator to Handle Discontinuities and Sharp Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19823)
*Ha Dang,Sebastian Schmidt,Juergen Hesser*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Cut-DeepONet提出两阶段训练框架，通过将问题提升到高维空间，显式建模间断为区域边界，避免直接逼近间断，在低分辨率数据下仍优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 神经算子在学习PDE解算子时表现优异，但其连续表示难以处理间断和剧烈变化，现有方法需增加模型容量和高分辨率数据。

Method: 采用lifting策略，将域划分为光滑子区域，将间断表示为高维空间中的边界；额外网络预测输入相关的间断位置，引导神经算子生成各区域内的光滑分量。

Result: 在基准PDE问题上，Cut-DeepONet优于最新方法，即使在低分辨率数据集上训练也能取得最佳效果，且使用更少的可训练参数。

Conclusion: 改变算子学习的表示方式比增加模型复杂度更有效，显式建模间断降低了学习难度。

Abstract: Neural operators have achieved strong performance in learning solution operators of partial differential equations (PDEs), but their inherently continuous representations struggle to capture discontinuities and sharp transitions. Existing approaches typically approximate such features within continuous function spaces, often requiring increased model capacity and high-resolution data. In this work, we propose Cut-DeepONet, a two-stage training framework that explicitly models discontinuities while reducing learning complexity. Our approach reformulates the problem via a lifting strategy, partitioning the domain into smooth subregions while representing discontinuities as boundaries in a higher-dimensional space. This separation aligns the operator learning task with the inductive bias of neural networks and avoids directly approximating discontinuities. An additional network predicts input-dependent discontinuity locations for unseen inputs, which are then used to guide the neural operator in generating smooth components within each region. Experiments on benchmark PDEs show that Cut-DeepONet outperforms state-of-the-art methods, even when trained on low-resolution datasets. The method excels on problems with discontinuities and sharp transitions, while using fewer trainable parameters. Our results highlight the benefits of changing the representation of operator learning rather than increasing model complexity.

### [152] [Symmetry in the Wild: The Role of Equivariance in Neural Fluid Surrogates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18816)
*Patryk Rygiel,Julian Suk,Kak Khee Yeung,Christoph Brune,Jelmer M. Wolterink*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了群等变架构在神经CFD代理（如AB-GATr）中的适用条件，发现当数据集存在强分布对齐（破缺对称性）时，等变性会损害分布内性能；但在几何多样、对齐较弱的血流动力学任务中，等变性持续有益，且显式等变始终优于数据增强的隐式对称学习。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 神经代理在CFD应用中需解决扩展到大规模网格、有限训练数据等问题。群等变架构能引入归纳偏置，但若学习问题本身破缺对称性（如数据集存在强分布对齐），等变性可能适得其反。本文旨在系统研究等变性在不同对齐程度和现实性任务中提升泛化能力的条件。

Method: 提出Anchored-Branched Geometric Algebra Transformer (AB-GATr)，一种融合可扩展性与对称性保持的E(3)-等变神经代理，能够高效建模耦合的表面和体积量。通过在汽车空气动力学和血流动力学（血液流动）任务上进行系统性实验，比较等变性与非等变架构、显式等变与数据增强隐式学习的性能。

Result: 在强对齐的空气动力学数据集中，强制等变性会降低分布内性能；在几何多样、对齐较弱的血流动力学基准中，等变性始终有益。在所有基准中，AB-GATr的显式等变性可靠地优于数据增强的隐式对称学习。

Conclusion: 等变性并非在所有领域普遍有益，但在缺乏强数据规律性的问题中能带来切实优势。

Abstract: Neural surrogates enable orders-of-magnitude acceleration of computational fluid dynamics (CFD) simulations, with the potential to transform engineering and healthcare workflows. Neural surrogate use in real-world applications requires addressing scalability to large, high-resolution surface and volume meshes, as well as to bespoke architectures, and accounting for limited training data through the use of inductive biases. Group-equivariant architectures are a principled way to introduce such bias, yet they can be detrimental when the learning problem itself breaks symmetry, for example, due to strong distributional alignment in the dataset. In this work, we investigate under which conditions equivariance improves generalization in neural CFD surrogates across tasks with increasing levels of distributional alignment and realism, covering automotive aerodynamics and blood flow (hemodynamics). To systematically assess the added value of equivariance at the limit of problem scaling, we introduce the Anchored-Branched Geometric Algebra Transformer (AB-GATr), a neural surrogate that integrates scalability and symmetry preservation to efficiently model coupled surface and volume quantities in an $E(3)$-equivariant manner. We find that on strongly aligned aerodynamics datasets, i.e., those that break symmetry, enforcing equivariance can degrade in-distribution performance. In contrast, across hemodynamic benchmarks with diverse geometries and varying alignment, equivariance is consistently beneficial. Moreover, across all benchmarks, the explicit equivariance of AB-GATr reliably outperforms implicit symmetry learning through data augmentation. Our findings showcase that equivariance is not universally beneficial across domains, yet it brings tangible advantages in problems lacking strong data regularities.

### [153] [Multi-Token Residual Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18817)
*Yufeng Xu,Zishuo Bao,Qian Wang,Zeshen Zhang,Haoqi Zhang,Bowen Peng,Ang Li,Rahul Chalamala,Yucheng Lu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Multi-token Residual Prediction (MRP)，利用扩散模型去噪过程中相邻步logit分布高度相似的特性，通过轻量模块从骨干网络隐藏状态预测步间残差，实现单次前向传播解码多个token，在SDAR模型上取得最高1.42倍无损加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有扩散语言模型(DLM)在解码时使用置信度阈值控制每步解码token数，但质量随每步解码token数增加而单调下降。作者希望在不显著增加计算成本的前提下，实现依赖感知的多token去噪，打破质量与速度之间的权衡。

Method: 提出Multi-token Residual Prediction (MRP)轻量模块。关键洞察是扩散模型去噪过程中相邻步的logit分布高度相似。MRP不重复运行骨干网络获取下一步logit，而是从骨干网络隐藏状态预测步间残差。支持两种推理模式：1) 直接解码（Direct Decoding）：使用校正后的logit直接解码，可调节质量-速度权衡；2) 推测解码（Speculative Decoding）：用骨干网络验证MRP的提案，实现无损加速。

Result: 在1.7B、4B、8B三个规模的SDAR模型上，在推理和代码生成基准测试中，使用SGLang实现最高1.42倍无损加速。

Conclusion: MRP通过预测残差替代额外前向传播，有效提升了扩散语言模型解码效率，且推测解码模式可保证无损加速，为DLM的实际部署提供了实用的加速方案。

Abstract: Diffusion Language Models (DLMs) generate text by iteratively denoising masked token sequences, offering a tradeoff between parallelism and quality compared to autoregressive models. In current practice, the number of tokens decoded per step is controlled by a confidence threshold, and quality degrades monotonically as more tokens are denoised per step. We introduce Multi-token Residual Prediction (MRP), a lightweight module that enables dependency-aware multi-token denoising within a single backbone forward pass. MRP exploits a key property of the denoising process: the logit distributions at adjacent denoising steps are remarkably similar. Rather than running the backbone a second time to obtain the next-step logits, MRP predicts the residual between steps from the backbone's hidden states, effectively denoising more tokens per backbone forward at a fraction of the cost. We deploy MRP in two inference modes: direct decoding, which uses the corrected logits without verification for a tunable quality--speed tradeoff; and speculative decoding, which verifies MRP's proposals against the backbone for lossless acceleration. Experiments on SDAR models at the 1.7B, 4B, and 8B scales across reasoning and code generation benchmarks demonstrate up to $1.42\times$ lossless speedup in SGLang.

Abstract: Constant Liar (CL), Kriging Believer (KB), and fantasy models are widely used for batch selection in parallel Bayesian Optimization, yet a unified theory explaining their effectiveness and conditions under which they fail has been lacking. We identify efficient conditioning as the key surrogate property the ability to update predictions in closed form when data is augmented. We prove that Gaussian Processes satisfy this requirement, producing provably distinct batch points with separation of order l, and that this holds for any acquisition function monotonically non decreasing in posterior uncertainty (EI, UCB, PI), with qualitatively similar behavior for Thompson Sampling. We unify CL, KB, and fantasy models as instances of a single conditioning mechanism differing only in the lie value distribution, and draw quantitative connections to Local Penalization (LP) and qualitative connections to Determinantal Point Processes (DPPs). To disentangle model structure from optimizer randomness, we introduce the Structural Diversity Diagnostic (SDD), a reusable methodology for testing surrogate compatibility. Experiments on Hartmann6D, Ackley 8D, Levy10D, and SVM hyperparameter tuning validate all theoretical predictions: CL or KBs implicit penalty matches or outperforms explicit LP greedy conditioning achieves convergence on par with joint qEI efficient conditioning extends to Multiquadric RBF networks; and parametric surrogates produce degenerate batches even when fully retrained (random forests), while neural networks regain diversity only at 15x the wall clock cost of GP conditioning. Robustness is confirmed across multiple initial datasets and under observation noise.

### [155] [Emergence of Frontier Superposition: Möbius attractor and Cascade Supervision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18820)
*Hongyu Gu,Jingwen Fu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文证明在Erdős-Rényi图上，通过Möbius吸引子（架构）和级联监督（损失设计）的组合，梯度下降能够学习到Transformer中的叠加推理（superposition reasoning），实现并行推理前沿，而端到端监督因梯度衰减而失败。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前工作（Zhu et al., 2025）手工构造了Transformer中利用叠加（superposition）实现并行推理的机制，但梯度下降能否在置换对称鞍点（permutation-symmetric saddles）中找到该目标是一个悬而未决的问题。

Method: 架构上识别出Möbius吸引子：在树状机制下，S_n-对称性使层间动力学退化为1D Möbius映射，其零集是包含等权叠加态的全局限优流形。监督上提出级联监督（Cascade Supervision），其反向传播同时提供选择性引导、跨深度梯度持久化和逐步骤判别。

Result: 端到端监督因内部梯度在深度c处衰减为(np)^{-(D-c-2)/2}而失败。实验验证：深度D=3时，端到端vs级联监督的最终步余弦相似度为0.35 vs 0.71（理论预测），实际为0.37 vs 0.69，每步误差在0.02以内。

Conclusion: Möbius吸引子+级联监督=叠加推理的涌现。该发现阐明了Transformer通过叠加进行深层推理的机制，并为训练此类模型提供了实用的监督策略。

Abstract: Superposition allows Transformers to reason in depth, carrying an entire reasoning frontier in parallel through a bounded-depth forward pass instead of unrolling serial chain-of-thought tokens. While Zhu et al. (2025) hand-crafted an equal-weight breadth-first frontier in a single residual stream for graph reachability, it remained open whether gradient descent could ever find this target amidst permutation-symmetric saddles.
  We close this gap on Reachability-by-Superposition over Erdős-Rényi graphs by isolating architectural and supervisional contributions. Architecturally, we identify a Möbius attractor: under $S_n$-symmetry in the tree regime, layerwise dynamics reduce to a 1D Möbius map whose zero set is a codimension-one manifold of global optima containing the equal-weight superposition state.
  On the supervision side, we identify Cascade Supervision: a loss class whose backward pass simultaneously delivers (A) selectivity bootstrap, (B) gradient persistence across depth, and (C) per-step discrimination (e.g., \mathcal{L}_{sup} and \mathcal{L}_{node}). End-to-end supervision fails condition (B) and is provably insufficient: internal gradients at layer c decay as (np)^{-(D-c-2)/2} in the graph fan-out and stall before the manifold is reached.
  Our thesis: Möbius attractor + Cascade Supervision = emergence of superposition reasoning. The parameter-free decay law predicts a final-step cosine of 0.35 vs. 0.71 (end-to-end vs. cascade) at depth D=3; experiments confirm 0.37 vs. 0.69, matching within 0.02 at every step.

</details>

### [160] [Not All Tokens Are Worth Caching: Learning Semantic-Aware Eviction for LLM Prefix Caches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18825)
*Shaoke Fang,Ziang Li,Wenfei Wu,Jiatong Ji,Qingsong Liu,Ruizhi Pu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SAECache 是一种语义自适应的前缀缓存淘汰策略，通过多队列架构、语义感知的令牌权重机制和完全自适应的在线学习方案，实现了 1.4-2.7 倍的 TTFT 提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有前缀缓存淘汰策略（如 LRU）将所有令牌块一视同仁，忽略了提示中不同令牌类型（系统提示、用户查询、工具输出、模型响应、思维链推理）的复用率差异可达 756 倍，导致缓存效率低下。

Method: 三个创新：(1) 多队列架构，按任务类型路由 KV 块并设置专用优先级指标；(2) 语义感知的令牌权重机制，通过淘汰反馈在线学习不同令牌类型的复用价值；(3) 完全自适应的在线学习方案，所有参数自动更新，无需手动调优。

Result: 在异构工作负载下，SAECache 相比生产级基线实现 1.4-2.7 倍 TTFT 提升，而固定参数替代方案在工作负载不匹配时性能可下降 2.7 倍。

Conclusion: 提出了一种无需手动调优、能自动适应部署工作负载特征的语义自适应前缀缓存淘汰策略，在广泛的工作负载下优于现有方法。

Abstract: Prefix caching is a key optimization in Large Language Model (LLM) serving, reusing attention Key-Value (KV) states across requests with shared prompt prefixes to reduce expensive prefill computation. However, its benefit depends critically on the eviction policy as GPU memory is scarce, and existing policies such as LRU largely treat cached blocks uniformly. This view ignores a fundamental property of LLM prompts: not all tokens are equally worth caching. We show that different token types within a prompt, including system prompts, user queries, tool outputs, model responses, and chain-of-thought reasoning, exhibit up to 756x variation in reuse rates, yet no existing eviction policy exploits this signal. In this paper, we present SAECache (Semantic-Adaptive Eviction for prefix caches), a semantic-adaptive prefix cache eviction policy that addresses this gap through three innovations: (1) a multi-queue architecture that routes KV blocks to task-specific queues with tailored priority metrics, capturing both session reuse in multi-turn requests and structural reuse in templated single-turn requests; (2) a semantic-aware token weighting mechanism that learns the reuse value of different token types online through eviction feedback; and (3) a fully adaptive online learning schema for all parameter updates, including log-normal timing parameters, position decay power, queue weights, and meta-parameters, which eliminates manual tuning and enables automatic adaptation to deployment-specific workload characteristics. Through extensive evaluation across heterogeneous workloads, we demonstrate that SAECache achieves 1.4x-2.7x TTFT improvement over production-style baselines, while fixed-parameter alternatives can degrade by up to 2.7x under workload mismatch -- a failure mode our adaptive approach avoids entirely.

</details>


### [161] [The Routing and Filtering Structure of Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18826)
*Shafayeth Jamil,Rehan Kapadia*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过分解注意力机制中的路由（routing）和过滤（filtering）成分，发现路由在低秩下运行，并提出S-D注意力参数化方法。该解耦方法揭示路由呈现谱级联现象，可预测注意力简化的可行性，并在多个规模模型上验证了有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准注意力机制中QK^T矩阵同时包含路由（位置间信息重新分配）和过滤（相互相关性缩放）两种纠缠计算，现有研究未能清晰解耦这两者，导致难以理解注意力的真实容量需求和简化方向。

Method: 1) 对1776个注意力头进行路由/过滤分解分析；2) 提出S-D注意力参数化，通过构造分离路由与过滤，保证稳定性；3) 在6种规模(7M-355M)模型上观察路由的谱级联现象；4) 基于级联预测简化注意力层。

Result: 路由在低秩下运行，远低于权重核分配的路由容量；路由自组织为谱级联，首层有效秩为2并随深度扩展；线性化前7层仅增加<5%困惑度，而标准注意力完全崩溃；级联分配的架构可节省47%-65%注意力参数。

Conclusion: 路由-过滤分解使注意力的谱预算更清晰，谱级联使简化注意力成为可行策略，为高效注意力架构设计提供理论指导。

Abstract: The attention interaction matrix $QK^{\top}$ contains two entangled computations: a skew-symmetric component that redistributes information between positions (routing) and a symmetric component that scales mutual relevance (filtering). We decompose 1776 heads across five pretrained transformers and find routing operating at low rank, well below the routing capacity allocated by the weight kernel. We introduce $S$-$D$ attention as a diagnostic parameterization that disentangles routing from filtering by construction with guaranteed stability ($\mathrm{Re}(λ) \le 0$) and trains stably without layer normalization. When disentangled and unnormalized, routing self-organizes into a spectral cascade, effective rank $2$ at the first layer, expanding with depth across six scales from 7M to 355M parameters. The cascade predicts where attention can be simplified: linearizing the first seven layers of 125M $S$-$D$ attention costs ${<}5\%$ perplexity, whereas standard attention collapses under the same intervention. The linearizable region widens with depth. Replacing the first four layers with ELU+1 linear attention reaches within $1.4\%$ of baseline at full head dimension. Cascade-allocated architectures trade attention parameters for perplexity ($47\%-65\%$ fewer attention parameters at $+3.9\%$ to $+8.4\%$ PPL). The routing-filtering decomposition makes the spectral budget legible; the cascade makes it actionable.

### [162] [Lossless Anti-Distillation Sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18829)
*Zibo Diao,Jingchu Gai,Xinyue Ai,Zhang Zhang,Zhenyu He,Di He*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 论文提出 Lossless Anti-Distillation Sampling (LADS)，一种在保持良性用户体验无损的前提下，通过基于语义内容和查询次数的私有种子生成随机性，使蒸馏者跨账号收集的数据产生相关性，从而恶化蒸馏模型泛化性能的新型采样方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前沿商业生成模型面临蒸馏攻击威胁，现有防御要么牺牲输出质量（修改模型输出），要么依赖行为检测（易被多账号绕过），缺乏既能保持良性用户体验又能有效对抗多账号蒸馏的方法。

Method: LADS 方案：每次生成时，随机性来自一个由查询语义内容和用户查询次数共同决定的私有种子。良性用户每次访问独立采样于原始模型，体验无损；蒸馏者不同账号在相同语义桶内共享潜在随机性，导致收集数据产生相关性。

Result: 理论证明 LADS 在无条件与条件生成下均能恶化蒸馏者的泛化差距收敛速率；实验表明在图像生成、数学推理和代码生成任务上，LADS 显著降低蒸馏学生模型性能，同时保持对单个用户的精确统计保真度。

Conclusion: LADS 提供了一种新型、轻量、无损的防御范式，在不牺牲良性用户体验的前提下通过引入数据相关性有效对抗多账号蒸馏攻击。

Abstract: Frontier commercial generative models face a growing threat from distillation, whereby a distiller harvests generated responses and trains a competing model of its own at drastically lower cost. Existing defenses either rely on modifying the models outputs, thereby sacrificing response quality for benign users, or on behavioral detection methods, which can be readily circumvented by distributing queries across multiple accounts. In this work, we propose Lossless Anti-Distillation Sampling (LADS), a novel sampling scheme specifically designed to counter multi-account distillation while maintaining a lossless experience for benign users. Concretely, LADS derives the randomness underlying each generation from a private seed determined by the semantic content of the query and the number of times the user has queried the model. By construction, every benign user receives a response independently sampled from the original model at each visit, and thus experiences no distortion. In contrast, for a distiller, different accounts share latent randomness whenever their queries fall in the same semantic bucket. As a result, the harvested data becomes correlated, potentially reducing sample diversity and degrading generalization. Using uniform convergence theory, we show that LADS provably degrades the convergence rate of the distillers generalization gap relative to standard i.i.d. sampling in both unconditional and conditional generation settings. Experiments on image generation, mathematical reasoning, and code generation confirm that LADS substantially degrades the performance of distilled students while preserving exact statistical fidelity for individual users.

### [163] [In-Context Learning Operates as Concept Subspace Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18830)
*Wei Tang,Xinyan Jiang,Fakhri Karray,Lijie Hu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过概念子空间视角研究上下文学习，发现任务信息可压缩到低维概念子空间中。在Llama-3-8B上，68-73维子空间（总4096维）恢复了78.8%的准确率差距，而补全其余子空间效果为零。概念交换能导向预测，随机控制无效。实验结果支持ICL通过紧凑、任务对齐的概念子空间中介可恢复行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已有研究表明ICL可以从演示中诱导预测器，且机制分析发现存在紧凑的激活方向可以引导行为，但结构化演示是否诱导低维概念推理仍不清楚。本文旨在通过概念子空间视角回答这一问题。

Method: 提出概念子空间视角：任务沿内在概念坐标变化，输入在高维观测空间中被观察。对于岭回归和最小二乘ICL代理，预测可精确分解为概念坐标回归和子空间泄露。在块对角或近块对角协方差假设下，主导项随概念子空间维度缩放，残差受跨子空间耦合控制。在CounterFact多关系提示上用Llama-3-8B、Qwen2.5-7B及跨语言规则任务进行实验验证。

Result: 在Llama-3-8B上，68-73维概念子空间（总4096维）恢复了78.8%的干净-损坏准确率差距，补全互补子空间效果为0%。概念交换能注入目标关系，随机和跨任务匹配秩控制无效。Qwen2.5-7B和跨语言规则任务呈现相同定性模式。

Conclusion: 概念子空间作为紧凑、任务对齐的ICL可恢复行为中介得到支持，但不意味着完整电路恢复。

Abstract: Regression and Bayesian accounts of in-context learning (ICL) explain how demonstrations can induce predictors, while mechanistic analyses often identify compact activation directions that steer prompted behavior. However, it remains unclear whether structured demonstrations induce low-dimensional concept inference. We study this question through a concept-subspace view of ICL, in which tasks vary only along intrinsic concept coordinates, although inputs are observed in a high-dimensional ambient space. For ridge and least-squares ICL proxies, prediction decomposes exactly into concept-coordinate regression and off-subspace leakage. Under block-diagonal or near-block-diagonal covariance assumptions, the leading estimation and nuisance-sensitivity terms scale with the dimension of the concept subspace, while residual effects are controlled by cross-subspace coupling. This separation gives a mechanistic prediction: recoverable task information should concentrate in a low-dimensional, task-aligned activation subspace. On CounterFact-derived multi-relation prompts with Llama-3-8B, a 68--73-dimensional subspace of the 4096-dimensional residual stream restores 78.8% of the clean--corrupted accuracy gap, whereas patching the complementary subspace restores 0%. Concept swaps redirect predictions toward injected relations, while random and cross-task matched-rank controls are largely ineffective. Additional experiments on Qwen2.5-7B and a controlled cross-lingual rule task show the same qualitative pattern. These results support concept subspaces as compact, task-aligned mediators of recoverable ICL behavior in structured task families, without implying full-circuit recovery.

*Bo Long,Deepak Agarwal,Jelena Markovic-Voronov,Yi Wang,Liuqing Li*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出BFT：注意力变为精度加权克里金法；残差连接变为带自适应增益的卡尔曼更新；FFN变为通过雅可比加过程噪声规则传播精度的动态模型；观测精度通过无参数REML估计器配合共轭贝叶斯先验得到，可即插即用替换任意Transformer层。

Abstract: The Transformer is the foundational building block of modern AI, yet offers no principled handling of \emph{uncertainty}, which is prevalent in real applications: cold-start tokens with sparse histories in sequential recommendation, heterogeneous signal quality in language models, and attention sinks induced by unconstrained softmax. Every token is treated with uniform confidence. We show this uniformity is a degenerate case of our \emph{Bayesian Filtering Transformer} (BFT): attention becomes precision-weighted kriging, the residual connection becomes a Kalman update with adaptive gain, and the FFN becomes a dynamics model propagating precision via a Jacobian--plus--process-noise rule. Observation precision comes from a parameter-free Restricted Maximum Likelihood (REML) estimator with a conjugate Bayesian prior. BFT replaces any Transformer layer with negligible overhead. On sequential recommendation, BFT applied to three major architectures yields significant gains on six benchmarks, with the largest improvements on cold-start users and rare items where uncertainty is highest. On supervised fine-tuning of large language models with noisy data, BFT improves robustness in two regimes: noisy supervision (token-label corruption in question answering) and noisy context (retrieval-augmented QA with real RAG distractors). A single principled modification -- restoring precision -- unlocks substantial headroom across both classical sequence-modeling and modern LLM regimes.

### [166] [StampFormer: A Physics-Guided Material-Geometry-Coupled Multimodal Model for Rapid Prediction of Physical Fields in Sheet Metal Stamping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18835)
*Jiajie Luo,Mohamed Mohamed,Osama Hassan,Haosu Zhou,Yingxue Zhao,Haoran Li,Xinrun Li,Zhutao Shao,Yang Long,Nan Li,Jichun Li*

Compared with ground truth FEA, our model achieved an average relative error of less than 8.5% on the four 2D fields and a mean squared error of less than 1.2 mm2 for the 3D displacement field. ### [167] [Spectral Gradient Surgery for Domain-Generalizable Dataset Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18836)
*Minyoung Oh,Najeong Chae,Jae-Young Sim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出领域泛化数据集蒸馏（DGDD）问题，针对分布匹配（DM）方法在分布外（OOD）场景下失效的问题，提出谱梯度手术（SGS）方法，通过解耦类别判别信息和领域特定信息，显著提升蒸馏数据集的OOD泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数据集蒸馏方法假设训练与测试数据同分布，但实际中常违反；直接套用后验领域泛化方法不适用于紧凑的合成数据集，且带来额外计算开销，违背蒸馏的效率目标。

Method: 提出谱梯度手术（SGS），利用谱域中跨域梯度的对齐关系，识别共享的类别判别成分（跨域一致）与领域特定成分（跨域分歧），通过增强共享成分和显式鼓励多样性两个互补梯度来改进标准DM更新。

Result: 在多种规模基准上的大量实验表明，SGS显著提升了OOD泛化性能，且与现有DM方法即插即用兼容。

Conclusion: 本文首次正式定义了领域泛化数据集蒸馏问题，并通过解耦梯度成分的方式有效缓解了合成数据集的OOD脆弱性，为蒸馏数据集的实际部署提供了新思路。

Abstract: Dataset Distillation (DD) synthesizes a compact synthetic dataset that preserves the training utility of a full dataset. However, its standard formulation assumes that test data follow the same distribution as training data, an assumption that rarely holds in practice. A straightforward extension-applying post-hoc Domain Generalization (DG) techniques to distilled data-is ill-suited because existing DG methods rely on the natural diversity of real datasets, which compact synthetic sets inherently lack, while also incurring substantial augmentation overhead that conflicts with the efficiency objective of dataset distillation. To address this limitation, we introduce Domain Generalizable Dataset Distillation (DGDD), a new problem setting that explicitly targets out-of-distribution (OOD) generalization of distilled datasets. We study this problem through a widely adopted DD baseline of Distribution Matching (DM). We attribute the OOD vulnerability of DM to the entanglement of class-discriminative and domain-specific information within the compressed synthetic set, and propose Spectral Gradient Surgery (SGS) to disentangle the two. The key insight of SGS is that cross-domain agreement among domain-wise gradients in the spectral domain reveals which gradient components are shared across source domains-and are therefore class-discriminative-and which are domain-specific. Based on this observation, SGS augments the standard DM update with two complementary gradients: one that reinforces cross-domain shared components and another that explicitly promotes diversity within the distilled dataset. Extensive experiments on diverse-scale benchmarks demonstrate that SGS substantially improves OOD generalization while remaining plug-and-play compatible with existing DM methods.

</details>


### [168] [VCR: Learning Valid Contextual Representation for Incomplete Wearable Signals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18837)
*Yuxuan Weng,Wenhan Luo,Qijia Shao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出VCR框架，通过正交解缠和缺失感知专家混合，在可穿戴健康监测中有效应对模态缺失问题，减少幻觉，提升鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有可穿戴设备面临标注数据有限和传感器模态缺失的挑战，而现有自监督方法假设模态完整，缺失处理方法容易产生幻觉，降低模型鲁棒性。

Method: VCR框架包含两个核心组件：1）正交分词器，通过潜在流形校正和几何投影实现模态间的严格正交解缠，分离为共享语义和模态特有残差；2）缺失感知混合专家（MoE）骨干网络，自适应不同模态缺失模式。训练目标仅重构缺失模态的共享部分，避免生成不可推断的细节。

Result: 在多种健康监测任务上，VCR在模态完整、单模态缺失和多模态缺失场景下均显著优于强监督和自监督基线方法。

Conclusion: VCR通过正交解缠和缺失感知设计，有效缓解了模态缺失下的幻觉问题，为可穿戴健康监测中的模态不完整问题提供了鲁棒的解决方案。

Abstract: Wearable devices enable continuous health monitoring from multimodal signals, but real-world deployment is hindered by limited labeled data and pervasive sensor incompleteness. While large-scale self-supervised pretraining reduces label dependence, most existing methods assume full modality availability. Current approaches for handling modality missingness often reconstruct entire absent signals, which can encourage hallucinating modality-specific details that are not inferable from the observed sensor signals and degrade robustness. We propose VCR, a self-supervised framework that learns to extract valid representations robust to modality missingness. VCR employs an orthogonal tokenizer to enforce strict orthogonal disentanglement by rectifying latent manifolds and applying a geometric projection, separating each modality into shared semantics and modality-specific residuals. This design preserves complete information integrity while serving as a structural foundation for robust learning under modality missingness. The resulting tokens are processed by a missing-aware mixture-of-experts backbone that adapts to varying patterns of modality availability. By constraining the objective to reconstruct only the shared components of missing modalities, VCR effectively mitigates hallucinations of non-inferable modality-specific details. Across multiple health monitoring tasks, VCR consistently improves performance and robustness under full, single-missing, and multiple-missing modality settings compared with strong supervised and self-supervised baselines.

</details>


### [169] [Lying Is Just a Phase: The Hidden Alignment Transition in Language Model Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18838)
*Adil Amin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了63个基础模型中推理能力与真实性的耦合关系，发现了一个损失曲线无法显示的"相变"：在模型规模低于某个临界值（约3.5B参数）时，能力之间呈反相关；超过临界值后，能力转为协同。架构、数据策展和训练配方独立影响这一相变点。论文还提供了无需模型内部信息的诊断工具和干预建议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有缩放定律只能预测计算量带来的损失变化，但无法解释不同能力（如推理与真实性）之间的相互作用关系，这限制了对模型行为的理解和可控性。

Method: 对16个模型家族共63个基础模型进行推理能力与真实性的耦合度测量；使用稀疏回归ODE进行跨家族预测；分析注意力头竞争机制；开发无需模型内部信息的诊断方法。

Result: 发现相变临界点N_c≈3.5B参数；数据策展可将耦合度从0.025提升至0.830；Gemma-4以4B参数达到13B+标准训练模型的耦合水平（0.871）；宽度归一化可消除所有测试家族的反相关现象；38/40模型无竞争注意力头；ODE跨家族预测误差5.6%。

Conclusion: 模型能力之间的耦合存在清晰的相变行为，可通过多种干预手段（数据策展、增加宽度、基准轮换等）进行调控，且该诊断方法可推广到前沿模型。

Abstract: Scaling laws predict loss from compute but not how capabilities interact. We measure the coupling between reasoning and truthfulness across 63 base models from 16 families and find a regime change invisible to loss curves: below a family-dependent critical scale $N_c$, capabilities anticorrelate; above it, they cooperate. $N_c \approx 3.5$B parameters [2.9B, 13.4B] (bootstrap 95% CI), but model size is not the only variable that determines phase. Architecture, data curation, and training recipe each shift $N_c$ independently: curated training eliminated the coupling dip between Qwen generations ($0.025 \to 0.830$ at matched scale), Gemma-4 at 4B achieves coupling 0.871, characteristic of 13B+ standard-trained models, through distillation and architectural innovation, and Phi at 1B matches web-trained coupling at 10B through data curation alone. Width normalization eliminates the anticorrelation across all tested families, supporting an output-projection bottleneck. Internally, 38 of 40 models show zero competing attention heads. A sparse-regression ODE cross-predicts held-out Llama-2 at 5.6% error. The diagnostic requires no model internals -- only public benchmark scores across a model family. The cooperative regime extends to the frontier ($r = +0.72$, 34 models, 10 labs). Code, data, and an open-source activation-steering tool for any open-weight model are released alongside an interactive dashboard that diagnoses any model's coupling phase, suggests concrete interventions (data curation, width, benchmark rotation), and provides ODE scaling predictions, frontier diagnostics, and eigenstructure analysis: https://zehenlabs.com/cape/.

### [171] [The Growing Pains of Frontier Models: When Leaderboards Stop Separating and What to Measure Next](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18840)
*Adil Amin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过将SWE-bench和GPQA Diamond分数分解为种群耦合趋势和每个版本的残差（h场），分析了34个模型（2024-2026年）的能力协同关系。研究发现能力整体协同（r=+0.72），但不同实验室和时间点差异显著：DeepSeek从推理优先转向编码优先（15.9个百分点摆动），Google保持一致的推理侧重，Anthropic在编码和推理间振荡。论文提供了三级行动手册、每实验室测量优先级表、七个可证伪预测，以及交互式仪表板。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有排行榜将前沿模型的能力视为独立维度进行评估，但未能揭示各能力在不同版本间是相互增强还是此消彼长。作者认为，在前沿模型演进中，能力之间的相互作用才是更具信息量的信号，因此需要一种方法来诊断模型发布时对各类能力的侧重方向。

Method: 将每对（SWE-bench, GPQA Diamond）分数分解为种群耦合趋势和每个版本的残差（h场），通过h场的符号和大小诊断模型对编码与推理能力的侧重。对34个模型（来自10个实验室，2024-2026年）进行回归分析，并构建了ODE-based缩放预测和交互式仪表板。

Result: 整体能力协同系数r=+0.72（p<10⁻⁶），但不同实验室差异达5倍（Google 1.15 vs DeepSeek 0.23）。DeepSeek h场从+11.2降至-4.7（15.9个百分点摆动），Google保持一致性，Anthropic呈现振荡。6个开放权重模型在30-72B参数区间出现第二次能力转变。SWE-bench趋于饱和，而HLE和指令遵循保持区分度。2026年4月的5个版本验证了诊断方法的样本外有效性（r从+0.72升至+0.75）。

Conclusion: 能力协同不是静态的，而是级联演变的。作者提供了三级行动手册（定位、诊断、旋转）、每实验室测量优先级表、七个可证伪预测，以及交互式仪表板（含阶段分类、h场诊断、每实验室耦合轨迹、基准旋转指导等），为未来12个月的前沿模型发布提供诊断框架。

Abstract: Leaderboards rank frontier models on independent axes but do not reveal whether capabilities reinforce or trade off across releases -- and at the frontier, this interaction is the more informative signal. We decompose paired SWE-bench and GPQA Diamond scores into a population coupling trend and per-release residual ($h$-field) that diagnoses capability emphasis and identifies which measurement or stress test is most informative next. Across 34 models from 10 labs (2024--2026), capabilities cooperate ($r = +0.72$, $p < 10^{-6}$), but cooperation varies by lab and over time: DeepSeek reversed from reasoning-rich to coding-first ($h$: $+11.2 \to -4.7$, 15.9-pp swing); Google maintains consistent reasoning emphasis; Anthropic oscillates between coding excursions and recovery. Cooperation is not static -- it cascades. Six open-weight architectures confirm a second capability transition at 30--72B, and SWE-bench is now saturating while HLE and instruction-following retain discriminatory spread -- signaling the next axis rotation. We provide a three-level playbook (locate, diagnose, rotate), a per-lab measurement-priority table, and seven falsifiable predictions with timestamped criteria for the next 12 months of frontier releases. Per-lab coupling slopes vary $5\times$ (Google $1.15$ vs. DeepSeek $0.23$), quantifying how efficiently each recipe converts coding gains into reasoning. Five April 2026 releases confirm the diagnostic out of sample ($r$ rises from $+0.72$ to $+0.75$). An interactive dashboard provides phase classification with actionable recommendations, $h$-field diagnostics, per-lab coupling trajectories, ODE-based scaling predictions, benchmark rotation guidance, self-steering demo, and live tracking of all seven predictions: https://zehenlabs.com/cape/.
